$(window).load(function() {
    
        if (!wb.settings.isMobileDevice && !wb.settings.disableBackground) {
            var $leftBg = $('.left-bg'),
                $body = $('.main-content'),
                leftBackground = '',
                rightBackground = '',
                backgroundColor = '';
            
            if (leftBackground)
                $leftBg.css('background', leftBackground);
            if (rightBackground)
                $body.css('background', rightBackground);
            if (backgroundColor)
                $leftBg.css('background-color', backgroundColor);
        }
    

    
        (function ($) {
            var container = $('#brandVote');
            var redesignCatalog = $.fn.wildCatalog("isRedesign");

            var brandId = container.data('brandId');
            var data = {
                redesign: redesignCatalog
            };
            var url = '/favoritebrands/getvotes/' + brandId;
            $.post(url, data, function (html) {
                container.html(html);
            });
        })(jQuery);
    

    
        (function ($) {
            var $container = $(".j-recent-goods-container");
            var action = loadVisitedGoods;
            
            onScroll($container, '.visited', action);

            function loadVisitedGoods(container) {
                //console.log('loadVisitedGoods');
                $.post("/visitedgoods", { count: container.attr("data-count") }, function (html) {
                    container.html(html);
                    wb.carousel.renderProductPrices(container);
                }, "html");
            }

            function onScroll(container, eventNameSpace, action) {
                var eventName = 'scroll' + eventNameSpace;
                $(window).on(eventName, function () {
                    if (!wb.utils.isElementInViewport(container, true))
                        return;

                    $(window).off(eventNameSpace);
                    action(container);
                }).trigger(eventName);
            }
        })(jQuery);
    

    
            (function () {
                $.when(wb.utils.script.require(wb.settings.scripts.tagline, true)).done(function (v1) {
                    wb.tagline.init();
                });
            }());
